2025-04-15T08:35:01.8988515Z  --- Check KSM (kernel memory deduper) --- 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9025309Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9025506Z Memory de-duplication instructions
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9025779Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9025993Z You have kernel memory de-duper (called Kernel Same-page Merging,
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9026407Z or KSM) available, but it is not currently enabled.
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9026638Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9026772Z To enable it run:
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9026972Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9027134Z     echo 1 >/sys/kernel/mm/ksm/run
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9027595Z     echo 1000 >/sys/kernel/mm/ksm/sleep_millisecs
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9027939Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9028161Z If you enable it, you will save 40-60% of netdata memory.
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9028541Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9028705Z  --- Check apps.plugin --- 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9066442Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9066631Z apps.plugin needs privileges
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9066908Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9067188Z Since you have installed netdata as a normal user, to have apps.plugin collect
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9067854Z all the needed data, you have to give it the access rights it needs, by running
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9068616Z either of the following sets of commands:
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9068977Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9069196Z To run apps.plugin with escalated capabilities:
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9069804Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9070158Z     sudo chown root:docker "/tmp/install/netdata/usr/libexec/netdata/plugins.d/apps.plugin"
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9070863Z     sudo chmod 0750 "/tmp/install/netdata/usr/libexec/netdata/plugins.d/apps.plugin"
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9071747Z     sudo setcap cap_dac_read_search,cap_sys_ptrace+ep "/tmp/install/netdata/usr/libexec/netdata/plugins.d/apps.plugin"
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9072301Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9072419Z or, to run apps.plugin as root:
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9072617Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9072937Z     sudo chown root:docker "/tmp/install/netdata/usr/libexec/netdata/plugins.d/apps.plugin"
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9073623Z     sudo chmod 4750 "/tmp/install/netdata/usr/libexec/netdata/plugins.d/apps.plugin"
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9074021Z 
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9074269Z apps.plugin is performing a hard-coded function of data collection for all
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9074891Z running processes. It cannot be instructed from the netdata daemon to perform
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9075381Z any task, so it is pretty safe to do this.
2025-04-15T08:35:01.9075604Z
